<li>Ski</li>\n        <li>Snow</li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2 class=\"h3 article-title upper\">Beginner’s Guide to Splitboarding: Getting Educated and Staying Safe</h2>\n      <div      <li>Snow</li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2 class=\"h3 article-title upper\">Beginner’s Guide to Splitboarding: Getting the Gear</h2>\n      <div class=\"inner-overlay\">\n        <div
